pli_egoweaponactionbarview.2	<color=3>Using awakening energy</color>\nYou can gain awakening energy by attacking an enemy using your spirit weapon. When you hit the opponent enough times to reach 100/100, you will receive a one-time full charge on your spirit weapon. You can only use the skill, however, when the weapon has been used more than once. Using the skill will increase the level on the energy bar to 100, and you must use the skill before the energy bar reaches zero.\n\n<color=3>Re-cycling time limit</color>\nUsing the skill will cause the energy bar to clear. So until you recharge your energy bar, you will not be able to use the awakening skill.

Tax payments are due weekly, and two or more overdue payments will lead to eviction and loss of  the lease. pli_housespecificinfotab.13	The tax rate is the ratio used to determine housing taxes within a castle's residential district.
